User : Prefer Credit account

API : api_response api_response:account_check_api, api_result:success
Bot : api_call:check_balance_api, user_account:Credit
API : api_response api_response:account_balance_api, api_result:success, balance:8000
Bot : end_call your current balance for account is 8000
